    function mrdVidGroups(cname) {
      console.log(' - ccpa > preroll > init()');

      var name = cname + "=";
      var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
      var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
      for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
          c = c.substring(1);
        }
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
          var data = c.substring(name.length, c.length);
          var items = data.split('&');
          for(var j = 0; j <items.length; j++) {
            var item = items[j].split('=');
            if (item[0] == 'groups') {
              return item[1];
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }
      return "";
    }

        function mrdfpGroups(cname) {
          console.log(' - ccpa > gam > init()');

          var name = cname + "=";
          var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
          var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
          for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
              c = c.substring(1);
            }
            if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
              var data = c.substring(name.length, c.length);
              var items = data.split('&');
              for(var j = 0; j <items.length; j++) {
                var item = items[j].split('=');
                if (item[0] == 'groups') {
                  return item[1];
                  break;
                }
              }
            }
          }
          return "";
        }

                var dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

                
                bloxServiceIDs.push();
                

                if (__tnt.user.services){
                    var bloxUserServiceIDs = __tnt.user.services.replace('%2C',',').split(',');
                }

                // GTM tncms.subscription.paid_access_service_ids
                if(bloxServiceIDs){
                    dataLayer.push({'tncms':{'subscription':{'access_service_ids':bloxServiceIDs.toString()}}});
                }

                // GTM tncms.subscrption.user_service_ids
                if(bloxUserServiceIDs){
                    dataLayer.push({'tncms':{'subscription':{'user_service_ids':bloxUserServiceIDs.toString()}}});
                }
            });
  </script>

        <div class="tncms-block nav-weather" id="tncms-block-668779">
         <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
          var jsonData;

  function buildAlerts(macro, querytype, filter) {
    if (querytype == "state") {
      var jsonp_url = 'https://cdn-webhooks.meredithlmg.com/nws/state/'+filter+'/processJSON';
    } else if (querytype == "county") {
      var counties = encodeURI(filter);
      var jsonp_url = 'https://cdn-webhooks.meredithlmg.com/nws/counties/'+counties+'/processJSON';
    } else if (querytype == "hash") {
      var jsonp_url = 'https://s3.amazonaws.com/meredith-alexa/jsonp/'+filter+'.json';
    }

    $.ajax({
      url: jsonp_url,
      dataType: 'jsonp',
      jsonp: false,
      jsonpCallback: 'processJSON',
      timeout: 10000,
      success: uberAlerts,
      error: parseError
    });
  }

  function uberAlerts(json) {
    jsonData = json;
    if ($('#wx-widget-alerts').length) {
      countJSON(json);
    }
    if ($('#expandable-weather-block').length) {
      parseExpandable(json);
    }
    if ($('#mrd-wx-alerts').length) {
      parseAlertJSON(json);
    }
  }

  function parseError() {
    console.log("/***********************************************");
    console.log("Severe Wx Retrieval Error: Please check JSONP");
    console.log("/***********************************************");
  }

  
  function countJSON(json) {

    
    alertCount = 0;
    $.each(json.alerts, function(key, val) {
      alertCount++;
      $("#wx-widget-alerts").show();
    });
    if (alertCount > 0 ) {
      var alertSuffix = (alertCount > 1 ? 's' : ''); 
      $("#wx-widget-alert-text").html(alertCount+" <span class=\"wxWidgetHide\">Weather</span> Alert"+alertSuffix).show();
    }

  }

  
  function parseExpandable(json) {

    
    alertCount = 0;
    $.each(json.alerts, function(key, val) {
      alertCount++;
      $("#expandable-weather-block .alert_count").text(alertCount);
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body ").append('<div id="mrd-alert'+ alertCount+ '"></div>');
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append("<h2>"+val.title+"</h2>");

      if (val.poly != "" && val.polyimg != "") {
        $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append('<img src="'+val.polyimg+'" alt="'+val.title+'" style="width:100%;/>');
      } else if (val.fips != "" && val.fipsimg != "") {
        // $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append('<img src="'+val.fipsimg+'" alt="'+val.title+'" style="width:100%;/>');
      }
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append(val.dhtml+"<p><b>"+val.ihtml+"</b></p>");
      $("#expandable-weather-block .weather-index-alerts").show();

      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body h2").css({"font-family":"'Fira Sans', sans-serif", "font-weight":"500", "padding-bottom":"10px"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body p").css({"font-size":"14px", "line-height":"24px"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body span.wxalertnum").css({"float":"left", "width":"40px", "height":"40px", "color":"#ffffff", "line-height":"40px", "background-color":"#888888", "border-radius":"40px", "text-align":"center", "margin-right":"12px"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body b").css("font-size", "18px");
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body li").css({"font-size":"14px", "line-height":"18px", "margin-bottom":"10px"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body ul").css({"margin-bottom":"24px"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body pre").css({"margin-bottom":"24px"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body img").css({"width":"100%", "margin-bottom":"20px", "borderWidth":"1px", "border-style":"solid", "border-color":"#aaaaaa"});
      $("#expandable-weather-block .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).css({"borderWidth":"0", "border-bottom-width":"1px", "border-style":"dashed", "border-color":"#aaaaaa", "padding-bottom":"10px", "margin-bottom":"40px"});

    });
  }

  
  function parseAlertJSON(json) {
    console.log(json);

    
    alertCount = 0;
    if (Object.keys(json.alerts).length > 0) {
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body ").empty();
    }
    $.each(json.alerts, function(key, val) {
      alertCount++;
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .alert_count").text(alertCount);
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body ").append('<div id="mrd-alert'+ alertCount+ '"></div>');
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append("<h2>"+val.title+"</h2>");

      if (val.poly != "" && val.polyimg != "") {
        $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append('<img src="'+val.polyimg+'" alt="'+val.title+'""/>');
      } else if (val.fips != "" && val.fipsimg != "") {
        // $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append('<img src="'+val.fipsimg+'" alt="'+val.title+'"/>');
      }

      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).append(val.dhtml+"<p><b>Instruction</b></p>"+val.ihtml);
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts").show();

      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body h2").css({"font-family":"'Fira Sans', sans-serif", "font-weight":"500", "padding-bottom":"10px"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body p").css({"font-size":"14px", "line-height":"24px"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body span.wxalertnum").css({"float":"left", "width":"40px", "height":"40px", "color":"#ffffff", "line-height":"40px", "background-color":"#888888", "border-radius":"40px", "text-align":"center", "margin-right":"12px"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body b").css("font-size", "18px");
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body li").css({"font-size":"14px", "line-height":"18px", "margin-bottom":"10px"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body ul").css({"margin-bottom":"24px"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body pre").css({"margin-bottom":"24px"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body img").css({"width":"100%", "margin-bottom":"20px", "borderWidth":"1px", "border-style":"solid", "border-color":"#aaaaaa"});
      $("#mrd-wx-alerts .modal-body #mrd-alert"+ alertCount).css({"borderWidth":"0", "border-bottom-width":"1px", "border-style":"dashed", "border-color":"#aaaaaa", "padding-bottom":"10px", "margin-bottom":"40px"});
    });
  }

  // Check if String or Object
  function check(obj) {
    if (typeof obj == 'string'){
      return String(obj);
    } else {
      return "";
    }
  }
         </script>

  <script>
   __tnt.trackEvent = function(obj) {
            if (typeof obj === 'object') {
                    if (obj.category && obj.action) {
                        __tnt.googleEvent(obj);
                    } else if (obj.network && obj.socialAction) {
                        __tnt.googleSocial(obj);
                    } else if (obj.url) {
                        __tnt.googlePageView(obj);
                    }
                    if (typeof TNCMS.Tracking != 'undefined' && obj.metric) {
                        TNCMS.Tracking.addEvent({
                            app: obj.app,
                            metric: obj.metric,
                            id: obj.uuid
                        });
                    }
            }
        };

        if (__tnt.trackEventLater.length > 0) {
            __tnt.trackEventLater.forEach(function(obj) {
                __tnt.trackEvent(obj);
            });
        }

        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-track]')).forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener(__tnt.client.clickEvent, function() {
                __tnt.trackEvent(JSON.parse(el.dataset.track));
            });
        });
        Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('body [data-tncms-track-event]')).forEach(function(el) {

  <script>
   $(function() {
    $('.asset-header .meta ul li:has(span.tnt-byline)').css('display', 'block');

    $(window).on('load', function() {
      $(' .meredith-summary-item > article ').each(function() {
        if ( $( this ).find(' div.tnt-video-container.video-responsive .f59-main:empty ').length ) {
          $( this ).find(' .mrd-container .mrd-image .media-preview ').css('z-index', '10');

$(document).ready(function(){
    // Set behavior for Cookie List reveal
    $('#cookieClose').on( "click", function() {
        $('#cookieInfo').hide();
    });
    function showCookieList() {
        $('#cookieInfo').show();
    }
    function getCcpaGroups(cname) {
      var name = cname + "=";
      var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
      var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
      for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
          c = c.substring(1);
        }
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
          var data = c.substring(name.length, c.length);
          var items = data.split('&');
          for(var j = 0; j <items.length; j++) {
            var item = items[j].split('=');
            if (item[0] == 'groups') {
              return item[1];
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }
      return "";
    }

    var ccpi_cat = getCcpaGroups("OptanonConsent");
    //console.log(' - ccpa > prep > get > group '+ccpi_cat);

    if (ccpi_cat.search(/,4:1/) >= 0) {
        $("script[class='targeted-enabled']").each(function(key, val){
            //console.log(' - ccpa > prep > set > rewrite targeted element #'+(key+1));

            var foo = $(val);
            if (foo.attr('type') === 'text/plain') {

              var s = document.createElement("script");
              s.type = "text/javascript";
              s.innerHTML = foo.text();

              $("head").append(s);
              $(s).addClass("targeted-enabled");

              foo.remove();
            }
        });
        $("script[class='targeted-disabled']").each(function(key, val){
          if ($(val).attr('type') === 'text/plain') {
            val.remove();
            //console.log(' - ccpa > prep > set > remove non-targeted element #'+(key+1));
          }
        });
    } else {
        $("script[class='targeted-disabled']").each(function(key, val){
            //console.log(' - ccpa > prep > set > rewrite non-targeted element #'+(key+1));

            var foo = $(val);
            if (foo.attr('type') === 'text/plain') {

              var s = document.createElement("script");
              s.type = "text/javascript";
              s.innerHTML = foo.text();

              $("head").append(s);
              $(s).addClass("targeted-disabled");

              foo.remove();
            }
        });
        $("script[class='targeted-enabled']").each(function(key, val){
          if ($(val).attr('type') === 'text/plain') {
            val.remove();
            //console.log(' - ccpa > prep > set > remove targeted element #'+(key+1));
          }
        });
    }
});
